-- РЎС‚СЂСѓРєС‚СѓСЂР° С‚Р°Р±Р»РёС†С‹ `chairs`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `chairs` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `code` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `title` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `pub` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=5 DEFAULT CHARSET=cp1251 AUTO_INCREMENT=5 ;

-- 
-- РЎС‚СЂСѓРєС‚СѓСЂР° С‚Р°Р±Р»РёС†С‹ `corriculums`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `corriculums` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `cycle_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `discipline_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `specialite_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `hours_auditory` int(11) default '0',
  `hours_lection` int(11) default '0',
  `hours_practice` int(11) default '0',
  `hours_laboratory` int(11) default '0',
  `hours_independent` int(11) default '0',
  `hours_exams` int(11) default '0',

-- РЎС‚СЂСѓРєС‚СѓСЂР° С‚Р°Р±Р»РёС†С‹ `kadri`
--

  `id` int(1) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `photo` varchar(100) collate cp1251_bin NOT NULL default '' COMMENT 'С„РѕС‚Рѕ',
  `fio` varchar(60) character set cp1251 NOT NULL COMMENT 'Р¤РРћ',
